### Critical revision targets before session 25

**1. Entity1 state carry-over (HIGH PRIORITY)**

@BELIEF:LAT80LON-20 is now **contradicted** (conf:40, contradiction_flag:true). The prior "state resets to 0 at new level" belief is wrong. @BELIEF:LAT90LON-30 (conf:240) replaces it: **state 1 carries over from a level WIN.**

**What this means for level 2**: The cross at rows 46–48 cols 50–52 is almost certainly unnecessary. Entity1 is already at state 1 when level 2 starts. The entire far-right track detour can be skipped.

**Revision needed in @LAT20LON-30**: The "Cross IS required for level 2 win" note (under State changers) is now contradicted by two consecutive session observations (23 and 24). Should be flagged as likely wrong.

---

**2. Trail attraction mechanic at state 1 (MEDIUM PRIORITY)**

@BELIEF:LAT10LON10 is **partially confirmed** (conf:155) but the mechanism is imprecisely understood. Current model:

- When trail column ≠ block column → action 0 (UP) moves *toward* trail column instead of NORTH
- When trail column = block column → UP moves normally NORTH

The @BELIEF:LAT80LON-30 route (19-action hypothesis) depends on trail column alignment being safe for the UP chain. The projected route keeps trail aligned at each step, but this has not been validated. **This is the most actionable unknown** — one bad redirect wastes an action and may strand the block.

**What to verify in session 25**: After the first UP (r40–41 → r35–36, trail aligns), does RIGHT from r35–36 c29–33 → c34–38 execute normally? Trail would be at c29–33 during that RIGHT step (1-step lag). Confirm the direction of any anomaly.

---

**3. Entity2 approach corridor (MEDIUM PRIORITY)**

@BELIEF:LAT80LON-30 proposes the winning route:

```
UP → RIGHT → UP×5 → LEFT×5 → DOWN×6 → RIGHT = 19 actions
```

Two structural assumptions not yet validated for this specific path with state 1 carry-over:
- Left track (c9–13) passable for DOWN×6 from rows 10–11 to rows 40–41 — confirmed session 11, but that was state 0
- Final RIGHT from c9–13 → c14–18 at r40–41 — state 1, trail column unknown at that point; attraction risk

The 11-ring A wall at rows 16–18 c15–17 **does not obstruct c9–13** (wall is 3 cols wide: 15, 16, 17; bypass is cols 9–13). Confirmed structurally in @BELIEF:LAT10LON0.
